SELECT `w`.`id`, `w`.`Date_created`, `w`.`Date_updated`, `w`.`is_active`, `w`.`occupation`, `w`.`User_id`, `u`.`id`, `u`.`birthdate`, `u`.`Date_created`, `u`.`Date_updated`, `u`.`description`, `u`.`email`, `u`.`first_name`, `u`.`gender`, `u`.`has_premium`, `u`.`is_active`, `u`.`last_name`, `u`.`password`, `u`.`phone_number`, `u`.`profile_pic`, `u`.`user_role`, `c`.`id`, `c`.`certificate_name`, `c`.`Date_created`, `c`.`Date_updated`, `c`.`imgUrl`, `c`.`institution_name`, `c`.`is_active`, `c`.`issue_date`, `c`.`name`, `c`.`teacher_name`, `c`.`Worker_id`, `s`.`id`, `s`.`content`, `s`.`Date_created`, `s`.`Date_updated`, `s`.`is_active`, `s`.`Worker_id`, `p`.`id`, `p`.`Date_created`, `p`.`Date_updated`, `p`.`image_url`, `p`.`is_active`, `p`.`Worker_id`, `r`.`id`, `r`.`date`, `r`.`Date_created`, `r`.`Date_updated`, `r`.`description`, `r`.`Employer_id`, `r`.`is_active`, `r`.`sent_by_id`, `r`.`Worker_id`
FROM `worker` AS `w`
INNER JOIN `users` AS `u` ON `w`.`User_id` = `u`.`id`
LEFT JOIN `certificates` AS `c` ON `w`.`id` = `c`.`Worker_id`
LEFT JOIN `skills` AS `s` ON `w`.`id` = `s`.`Worker_id`
LEFT JOIN `portfolio` AS `p` ON `w`.`id` = `p`.`Worker_id`
LEFT JOIN `reviews` AS `r` ON `w`.`id` = `r`.`Worker_id`
